[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn Out of Memory [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOOM[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m error occurs during fuzzing of PDF text extraction [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality. The Java heap space is exhausted when processing a PDF document, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically during the parsing of a PFB [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPrinter Font Binary[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m font file within the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mApache PDFBox library. The issue manifests when attempting to create a Type1Font [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom PFB data, triggered through the [0m[1;35mPDFTextStripper.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m operation.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis issue represents a resource exhaustion vulnerability where the application [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mruns out of memory while processing specially crafted input. The fuzzer detected [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis condition during the execution of [0m[1;35mPDFExtractTextFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich attempts to extract text from a PDF document.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe stack trace reveals a clear sequence of operations leading to the memory [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaustion:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer invokes [0m[1;35mPDFTextStripper.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m on a crafted PDF document[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. During page processing, a font resource needs to be loaded [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;35mSetFontAndSize.process[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mPDFontFactory.createFont[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is called to instantiate a font object[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. A PDType1Font is initialized, which requires creating a Type1Font from PFB data[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mPfbParser.parsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is invoked at line [0m[1;36m166[0m[39m, where the OutOfMemoryError is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthrown[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. The parser constructor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPfbParser.<init>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m at line [0m[1;36m116[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was in the process of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing the PFB data[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability type is classified as a Denial of Service [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDoS[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m through resource [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexhaustion, specifically marked as [0m[32m"FuzzerSecurityIssueLow"[0m[39m by the Jazzer fuzzing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mframework. The error occurs in the org.apache.fontbox.pfb.PfbParser class, which is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresponsible for parsing Printer Font Binary files.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant observations include:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The memory exhaustion occurs during font parsing rather than general PDF [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The specific failure point is at PfbParser.java line [0m[1;36m166[0m[39m within the [0m[1;35mparsePfb[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The error can be reproduced with a heap size of 1710MB [0m[1;39m([0m[39m-Xmx1710m flag[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The issue is triggered through normal PDF text extraction workflows, not through [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many exotic API usage[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo gain a holistic view of this issue, the following components should be [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvestigated:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **PfbParser.java** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m116[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m166[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The immediate failure point where memory[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation occurs. Understanding what data structures are being created and what [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize calculations are performed is critical.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Type1Font.java** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m69[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The [0m[1;35mcreateWithPFB[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m method that initiates the PFB [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing process. This may contain validation logic or size checks that could be [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbypassed.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **PDType1Font.java** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m227[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The font initialization code that triggers font[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreation, which may lack proper resource limits or validation.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **PDFontFactory.java** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m140[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: The factory method responsible for font [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcreation, which could be the appropriate place for implementing font size [0m          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetermine segment size[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Lines [0m[1;36m161[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m164[0m[39m**: The code checks if `total + size > MAX_LENGTH`, but this [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck validates the accumulated total, not the individual segment size[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m166[0m[39m**: `byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m ar = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39msize[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;` - **CRITICAL VULNERABILITY** - [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation happens with potentially malicious size value[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m172[0m[39m**: Only after allocation is `total` updated[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue is that even though there's a MAX_LENGTH check, it doesn't prevent an [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindividual segment from having an extremely large size [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., close to 2GB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocation at line [0m[1;36m166[0m[39m happens before the accumulated total is updated, allowing a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrafted PFB file to specify a segment size that directly causes OOM.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdditionally, the size reading using bitwise operations could result in negative [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues if the most significant byte [0m[1;39m([0m[39mMSB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is >= [0m[1;36m0x80[0m[39m, which would cause [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`NegativeArraySizeException` instead of OOM.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Implementation[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `fontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/pfb/PfbParser.java`[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Exact insertion point**: After line [0m[1;36m160[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter logging the size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and before line [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m161[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore calculating newTotal[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Validation code to add**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m After line [0m[1;36m160[0m[39m: [0m[1;35mLOG.debug[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"record type: [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m, segment size: [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m, recordType, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Add these lines before line [0m[1;36m161[0m[39m:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Invalid negative segment size: "[0m[39m + size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize > MAX_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Segment size "[0m[39m + size + [0m[32m" exceeds maximum allowed "[0m[39m + [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This Fix Is Optimal[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Validates before allocation**: The check happens after reading the size but [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore any memory allocation attempts, preventing both OOM and [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNegativeArraySizeException at the source.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Defense in depth**: Works in conjunction with the existing check at line [0m[1;36m162[0m[39m that[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidates accumulated total. Now we have:[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Individual segment validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnew[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Accumulated total validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexisting at line [0m[1;36m162[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Final allocation validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimplicitly at line [0m[1;36m182[0m[39m with validated total[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Follows existing patterns**: [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Similar to the existing MAX_LENGTH check at line [0m[1;36m162[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with error handling patterns throughout the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., CFFParser [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalidates offsets before allocation[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Matches the approach in other PDFBox parsers that validate sizes before [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocations[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Preserves all functionality**:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to PFB format parsing logic[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to segment reorganization algorithm[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to public API[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to the three constructors[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains the existing MAX_LENGTH constant [0m[1;39m([0m[39m100MB[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Clear error messages**: Provides descriptive error messages that distinguish [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbetween negative sizes and excessive sizes, aiding debugging and security analysis.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Impact Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Legitimate fonts**: All legitimate Type1 fonts will continue to work:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Test fonts in the codebase range from 100KB to 1MB[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- MAX_LENGTH is 100MB, providing ample headroom[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The largest known Type1 fonts are well under 100MB[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Malicious inputs**:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fonts with individual segments > 100MB: Rejected with clear error message[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fonts with negative size values: Rejected with clear error message[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fonts with accumulated size > 100MB: Rejected by existing check at line [0m[1;36m162[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- OOM vulnerability: Completely mitigated[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No breaking changes**:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing unit tests will pass [0m[1;39m([0m[39mverified by test analysis showing test fonts are [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m100KB-1MB[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Public API unchanged[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Font processing logic unchanged[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only adds validation, no behavioral changes for valid input[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential side effects**:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Extremely large legitimate fonts**: If a legitimate Type1 font exceeds 100MB, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mit will be rejected[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is extremely unlikely for Type1 fonts. If needed, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_LENGTH can be increased, but 100MB is already very generous for this format[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Malformed but non-malicious fonts**: Some damaged fonts might have incorrect [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize fields that now get rejected[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: This is actually desirable behavior - the current code would [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mOOM on such fonts anyway. The fix converts an OOM crash into a clean IOException [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith a descriptive message[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No mitigation needed for**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Compatibility: The fix only affects invalid/malicious input[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Performance: Validation adds negligible overhead [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtwo integer comparisons[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory usage: Reduces memory usage by preventing excessive allocations[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Alignment with Codebase Patterns[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar validation patterns found**:[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `RandomAccessReadMemoryMappedFile.jav[0m[1;92ma:84[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m88[0m[39m`: Validates size > [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInteger.MAX_VALUE before allocation[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `CFFParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:293[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m295[0m[39m`: Validates offset against input length before reading[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. `BaseParser.jav[0m[1;92ma:1450[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1454[0m[39m`: Validates accumulated length against [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_LENGTH_LONG[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. `ScratchFileBuffer.jav[0m[1;92ma:107[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m114[0m[39m`: Checks for integer overflow and maximum buffer[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Consistent error handling**:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Throws IOException with descriptive messages [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmatching existing pattern at line [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Logs at debug level before validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexisting pattern at line [0m[1;36m160[0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fails fast to prevent resource exhaustion[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Complete Fix from Initial Codebase[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSince this is the first patch attempt, the fix should be applied to the initial [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase at:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: `fontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/pfb/PfbParser.java`[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Line numbers**: Insert after line [0m[1;36m160[0m[39m, before line [0m[1;36m161[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix requires adding exactly [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m lines of code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding blank lines for [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreadability[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m blank line for separation[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m opening brace for first if statement[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m throw statement for negative size[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m closing brace[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m opening brace for second if statement  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m throw statement for excessive size[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m closing brace[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m blank line before existing line [0m[1;36m161[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis minimal change addresses the security vulnerability without modifying any [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mother functionality, maintaining backward compatibility while preventing [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdenial-of-service attacks through resource exhaustion.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
